<Review>Mediterranean food is good, but for me it's never been anything special. Food is special when it makes me feel special. I feel special when my food makes me feel like it's only us left on this Earth. When everything else in the background fades and the only thing clear in my life is my food, that's special. That's why I don't like eating out with people, especially if we're going to a nice place. Anyways, when my friends and I got food from SAJJ I didn't think I was going to have any trouble eating with them...how wrong I was. < review>
Looking at the copy of the adverstisement, I was interested in some of the produce and meat that were on special.  Though I am long time resident of Inland Empire.  This is the very first time visiting the Rio Ranch Market in Southern California.  Searched on line for the store locations.  Decided to visit Fontana store on Cherry Avenue around 5:50pm.  Parking lot was clean; shopping carts collected.  First impression as I entered, the store was clean and organized.  The floor waxed and shining. Shelves were stocked, zoned and no missing labels.  All advertised items are highlighted with proper and visible signage.  Decided to go down aisle by aisle and see the quality and products carried.  Cashier greeted me and security guard was friendly and helped me loading the bags onto shopping cart.  One of better grocery shopping experiences that I had in comparison to F4L and El Super.  Fontana will be my home store from here out.<//review>

Five hours to unload meat. One of, if not THE WORST,  dock set up I have seen in 20+ years. You will need to work with other drivers to drop thier/your trailer so people have enough room to back in.

Enter at gate #1 by Ralph's sign. Its the second entrance on right from Hwy 60. Have your safety vest on at check in.

If you have a door in the 300s (north side), take your paperwork to door 429 BEFORE going to your door. Or you will need to walk all the way around the building after getting parked.

They really just need to tell everyone to drop their trailer at the door and bobtail over to a holding area until called to pick up their trailer when it's empty.<//text>

<review>Not the best place to deliver, but also not as bad as is described in previous comments if you come prepared:
1. Have your safety vest. IMPORTANT: the one with reflective tape on it. Otherwise they won't even take your paperwork.
2. Security guards are not as rude as I thought. Arrived 1 day early. Was nicely explained that I cannot stay on the premises and adviced a place to park overnight.
3. Parking spots are very tight. Ask somebody to help you park if you don't want to call your insurance.
4. Unloading takes long
Appointment: 8 p.m.
Checked in: 7 p.m. (you can check in one hour early)
Parked at the dock: 10 p.m.
Unloaded: 2 a.m.
Six hours is a lot.
5. They leave mess in your trailer, but you can throw it in the dumpster by the gate.

Just come prepared that you will spend here some time and you will save yourself a lot of nerves.</review><Pics>None</Pics>< Response>

<Resp>None<//Resp><Review>Other than tight parking spots and iffy location, this place is no different than any other grocery  dc. Same rude guards, same expensive lumpers, and, the most important thing, yes, they are SLOW. In this case lumpers were somewhat quick to unload my trailer (I only had 4 pallets), but the receiver took almost 4 hours to accept product.

Do not come here early, 1 hour before your appointment time is the earliest they will let you in. But even then, it totally depends on parking availability at the staging area. If its full, they can still kick you out and tell you to come back at your appointment time. I saw some trucks parked on Wilmington right in front of the entrance. Well, you can try to park there, but chances are you will get a ticket. Its a no parking zone. There is some temporary parking on University Dr and also on Carson Street. Carson St is limited to 1 hour. I parked on Carson for about 4 hours and was lucky to not to get a ticket.

Now backing your trailer into a dock is another story. If you have anything bigger than daycab + 48' trailer, you are out of luck. I saw daycab with 53' taking off the mirror off the truck next to him. So, be prepared to practice your driving skills when you come here.< /Review>< rate>
